torch.Tensor:\n    \"\"\"Compute exclusive prefix-sum offsets from vocab_sizes.\n\n    Args:\n        vocab_sizes: Per-layer per-ngram embedding table sizes of shape\n            (num_ngram_layers, max_ngram_size - 1, num_embed_table_per_ngram), int32.\n\n    Returns:\n        Offsets of shape (num_ngram_layers, (max_ngram_size - 1) * num_embed_table_per_ngram), int32.\n    \"\"\"\n    num_ngram_layers = vocab_sizes.shape[0]\n    offsets_list = []\n    for layer_idx in range(num_ngram_layers):\n        flat = vocab_sizes[layer_idx].view(-1)\n        prefix = engram_hash_ref(\n    ngram_token_ids: torch.Tensor,\n    multipliers: torch.Tensor,\n    vocab_sizes: torch.Tensor,\n    offsets: torch.Tensor,\n) -> torch.Tensor:\n    \"\"\"Pure PyTorch reference implementation of engram hash.\n\n    Args:\n        ngram_token_ids: N-gram token IDs of shape (num_tokens, max_ngram_size), int32.\n        multipliers: Per-layer hash multipliers of shape (num_ngram_layers, max_ngram_size), int64.\n        vocab_sizes: Per-layer per-ngram embedding table sizes of shape\n            (num_ngram_layers, max_ngram_size - 1, num_embed_table_per_ngram), int32.\n        offsets: Per-layer embedding table offsets of shape\n            (num_ngram_layers, (max_ngram_size - 1) * num_embed_table_per_ngram), int32.\n\n    Returns:\n        Embedding indices of shape (num_ngram_layers, num_tokens, (max_ngram_size - 1) * num_embed_table_per_ngram), int32.\n    \"\"\"\n    num_ngram_layers = multipliers.shape[0]\n    max_ngram_size = multipliers.shape[1]\n\n    prod = ngram_token_ids.to(torch.int64).unsqueeze(0) * multipliers.unsqueeze(1)\n\n    ans = [[] for _ in range(num_ngram_layers)]\n    hashes = prod[:, :, 0].clone()\n    for i in range(1, max_ngram_size):\n        hashes.bitwise_xor_(prod[:, :, i])\n        for layer_idx in range(num_ngram_layers):\n            ans[layer_idx].append((hashes[layer_idx].unsqueeze(-1) % vocab_sizes[layer_idx, i - 1].to(torch.int64).unsqueeze(0)).to(torch.int32))\n\n    for layer_idx in range(num_ngram_layers):\n        ans[layer_idx] = torch.cat(ans[layer_idx], dim=-1)\n\n    output torch.Tensor,\n    weight_embed: torch.Tensor,\n    clamp_value: float,\n    eps: float,\n    save_for_backward: bool = False,\n) -> torch.Tensor | tuple[torch.Tensor, torch.Tensor, torch.Tensor, torch.Tensor, torch.Tensor]:\n    \"\"\"Pure PyTorch reference implementation of engram gate (vectorized, supports autograd).\n\n    Computes: output = x + sigmoid(signed_sqrt(dot(RMSNorm(x, wh), RMSNorm(k, we)) * scalar)) * v\n\n    Args:\n        hidden_states: Input of shape (num_tokens, hc_mult, hidden_size), bfloat16.\n        k: Key embeddings of shape (num_tokens, hc_mult, hidden_size), bfloat16.\n        v: Value embeddings of shape (num_tokens, hidden_size), bfloat16.\n        weight_hidden: RMSNorm weight for hidden states, shape (hc_mult, hidden_size), bfloat16.\n        weight_embed: RMSNorm weight for key embeddings, shape (hc_mult, hidden_size), bfloat16.\n        clamp_value: Clamp threshold for signed-sqrt gate activation.\n        eps: Epsilon for RMSNorm numerical stability.\n        save_for_backward: If True, also return (dot, gate_score, rstd_x, rstd_k).\n\n    Returns:\n        If save_for_backward is False: output tensor of shape (num_tokens, hc_mult, hidden_size), bfloat16.\n        If save_for_backward is True: tuple of (output, dot, gate_score, rstd_x, rstd_k).\n    \"\"\"\n    hidden_size = hidden_states.shape[-1]\n    scalar = hidden_size**-0.5\n\n    x = hidden_states.float()\n    k_f = k.float()\n    wh = weight_hidden.float().unsqueeze(0)\n    we = weight_embed.float().unsqueeze(0)\n\n    # RMSNorm\n    rstd_x = torch.rsqrt(x.pow(2).mean(-1) + eps)\n    rstd_k = torch.rsqrt(k_f.pow(2).mean(-1) + eps)\n\n    # Dot -> sqrt-gate -> sigmoid\n    # raw_dot is the unnormalized sum(x * wh * k * we), matching the kernel's dot_out\n    raw_dot = torch.einsum('...d,...d->...', x * wh, k_f * we)\n    dot = raw_dot * rstd_x * rstd_k * scalar\n    signed_sqrt = dot.abs().clamp_min(clamp_value).sqrt() * dot.sign()\n    gate_score = signed_sqrt.sigmoid()\n\n    output = x + gate_score.unsqueeze(-1) * v.unsqueeze(-2)\n    output = output.bfloat16()\n\n    if save_for_backward:\n        return output, raw_dot, T.Tensor[(num_tokens, hc_mult, hidden_size), T.bfloat16],\n        k: T.StridedTensor[(num_tokens, hc_mult, hidden_size), (k_stride_s, k_stride_h, 1), T.bfloat16],\n        v: T.StridedTensor[(num_tokens, hidden_size), (v_stride_s, 1), T.bfloat16],\n        weight_fused: T.Tensor[(hc_mult, hidden_size), T.float],\n        output: T.Tensor[(num_tokens, hc_mult, hidden_size), T.bfloat16],\n        dot_out: T.Tensor[(num_tokens, hc_mult), T.float],\n        gate_score: T.Tensor[(num_tokens, hc_mult), T.float],\n        rstd_x: T.Tensor[(num_tokens, hc_mult), T.float],\n        rstd_k: T.Tensor[(num_tokens, hc_mult), T.float],\n    ):\n        with T.Kernel(hc_mult, num_persistent_blocks, threads=threads) as (pid_h, pid_b):\n            thread_idx = T.get_thread_binding()\n            x_local = T.alloc_local((vec_size,), T.float)\n            k_local = T.alloc_local((vec_size,), T.float)\n            w_local = T.alloc_local((vec_size,), T.float)\n            v_local = T.alloc_local((vec_size,), T.float)\n            gate_score_local = T.alloc_local((1,), T.float)\n            rstd_x_local = T.alloc_local((1,), T.float)\n            rstd_k_local = T.alloc_local((1,), T.float)\n            gate_score_reducer = T.alloc_local((1,), T.float)\n            rstd_x_reducer = T.alloc_local((1,), T.float)\n            rstd_k_reducer = T.alloc_local((1,), T.float)\n\n            x_smem = T.alloc_shared((hidden_size,), T.bfloat16)\n            kv_smem = T.alloc_shared((2, blk_d), T.bfloat16)\n\n            per_block = T.ceildiv(num_tokens, num_persistent_blocks)\n            t_start = T.min(per_block * pid_b, num_tokens)\n            t_end = T.min(per_block * (pid_b + 1), num_tokens)\n\n            for i_s in T.Serial(t_start, t_end):\n                # === Pass 1: Reduction with cp.async pipeline ===\n                if i_s == t_start:\n                    T.async_copy(hidden_states[i_s, pid_h, 0:blk_d], x_smem[0:blk_d])\n                    T.async_copy(k[i_s, pid_h, 0:blk_d], kv_smem[0, :])\n\n                T.clear(rstd_k_local)\n                T.clear(rstd_x_local)\n                T.clear(gate_score_local)\n\n                for i_b in T.Serial(1, num_blk):\n                    phase = i_b % 2\n                    prev_phase = (i_b - 1) % 2\n                    T.async_copy(hidden_states[i_s, pid_h, i_b * blk_d:(i_b + 1) * blk_d], x_smem[i_b * blk_d:(i_b + 1) * blk_d])\n                    T.async_copy(k[i_s, pid_h, i_b * blk_d:(i_b + 1) * blk_d], kv_smem[phase, :])\n                    T.ptx_wait_group(2)\n                    for i_sub in T.Serial(sub_blks):\n                        sub_base = (i_b - 1) * blk_d + i_sub * reduce_blk\n                        for i_k in T.vectorized(vec_size):\n                            x_local[i_k] = x_smem[sub_base + thread_idx * vec_size + i_k]\n                            k_local[i_k] = kv_smem[prev_phase, i_sub * reduce_blk + thread_idx * vec_size + i_k]\n                        for i_k in T.vectorized(vec_size):\n                            w_local[i_k] = weight_fused[pid_h, sub_base + thread_idx * vec_size + i_k]\n                        for i_k in T.serial(vec_size):\n                            rstd_x_local[0] += x_local[i_k] * x_local[i_k]\n                            rstd_k_local[0] += k_local[i_k] * k_local[i_k]\n                            gate_score_local[0] += x_local[i_k] * w_local[i_k] * k_local[i_k]\n\n                # Epilogue: process last tile\n                T.ptx_wait_group(0)\n\n                # Prefetch v[0] into freed kv_smem bank\n                T.async_copy(v[i_s, 0:blk_d], kv_smem[v_start_phase, :])\n\n                for i_sub in T.Serial(sub_blks):\n                    sub_base = (num_blk - 1) * blk_d + i_sub * reduce_blk\n                    for i_k in T.vectorized(vec_size):\n                        x_local[i_k] = x_smem[sub_base + thread_idx * vec_size + i_k]\n                        k_local[i_k] = kv_smem[(num_blk - 1) % 2, i_sub * reduce_blk + thread_idx * vec_size + i_k]\n                    for i_k in T.vectorized(vec_size):\n                        w_local[i_k] = weight_fused[pid_h, sub_base + thread_idx * vec_size + i_k]\n                    for i_k in T.serial(vec_size):\n                        rstd_x_local[0] += x_local[i_k] * x_local[i_k]\n                        rstd_k_local[0] += k_local[i_k] * k_local[i_k]\n                        gate_score_local[0] += x_local[i_k] * w_local[i_k] * k_local[i_k]\n\n                # Prefetch v[1]\n                T.async_copy(v[i_s, blk_d:2 * blk_d], kv_smem[1 - v_start_phase, :])\n\n                rstd_k_reducer[0] = T.warp_reduce_sum(rstd_k_local[0])\n                rstd_x_reducer[0] = T.warp_reduce_sum(rstd_x_local[0])\n                gate_score_reducer[0] = T.warp_reduce_sum(gate_score_local[0])\n\n                rstd_x_reducer[0] = T.rsqrt(rstd_x_reducer[0] / hidden_size + eps)\n                rstd_k_reducer[0] = T.rsqrt(rstd_k_reducer[0] / hidden_size + eps)\n\n                if save_for_backward:\n                    if thread_idx == 0:\n                        dot_out[i_s, pid_h] = gate_score_reducer[0]\n                        rstd_x[i_s, pid_h] = rstd_x_reducer[0]\n                        rstd_k[i_s, pid_h] = rstd_k_reducer[0]\n\n                gate_score_reducer[0] = gate_score_reducer[0] * rstd_x_reducer[0] * rstd_k_reducer[0] * scalar\n\n                gate_score_reducer[0] = T.sigmoid(T.copysign(T.sqrt(T.clamp(T.abs(gate_score_reducer[0]), clamp_value, float('inf'))), gate_score_reducer[0]))\n\n                if save_for_backward:\n                    if thread_idx == 0:\n                        gate_score[i_s, pid_h] = gate_score_reducer[0]\n\n                # === Pass 2: Output — x from smem, v from kv_smem (tiles 0,1 already prefetched) ===\n                for i_b in T.Serial(num_blk):\n                    tile_phase = (v_start_phase + i_b) % 2\n                    if i_b < num_blk - 1:\n                        T.ptx_wait_group(1)\n                    else:\n                        T.ptx_wait_group(0)\n                        # Prefetch next token's k and x\n                        if i_s + 1 < t_end:\n                            T.async_copy(k[i_s + 1, pid_h, 0:blk_d], kv_smem[0, :])\n                            T.async_copy(hidden_states[i_s + 1, pid_h, 0:blk_d], x_smem[0:blk_d])\n                    for i_sub in T.Serial(sub_blks):\n                        sub_base = i_b * blk_d + i_sub * reduce_blk\n                        for i_k in T.vectorized(vec_size):\n                            x_local[i_k] = x_smem[sub_base + thread_idx * vec_size + i_k]\n                            v_local[i_k] = kv_smem[tile_phase, i_sub * reduce_blk + thread_idx * vec_size + i_k]\n                        for i_k in T.vectorized(vec_size):\n                            output[i_s, pid_h, sub_base + thread_idx * vec_size + i_k] = x_local[i_k] + gate_score_reducer[0] * v_local[i_k]\n                    # Prefetch v[i_b+2] into freed kv_smem bank\n                    if i_b + 2 < num_blk:\n                        T.async_copy(v[i_s, (i_b + 2) * blk_d:(i_b + 3) * blk_d], kv_smem[tile_phase, :])\n\n    return engram_gate_fwd_kernel\n\n\n@tilelang.jit(\n    pass_configs={\n        tilelang.PassConfigKey.TL_DISABLE_WARP_SPECIALIZED: True,\n        tilelang.PassConfigKey.TL_DISABLE_THREAD_STORAGE_SYNC: True,\n        tilelang.PassConfigKey.TL_DISABLE_OUT_OF_BOUND_WARNING: True,\n    },\n)\ndef get_engram_gate_bwd_kernel(\n    hidden_size: int,\n    scalar: float,\n    k_stride_s: int,\n    k_stride_h: int,\n    v_stride_s: int,\n    num_persistent_blocks: int,\n    clamp_value: float = 1e-6,\n    hc_mult: int = 4,\n):\n    \"\"\"Backward kernel: 8 warps per CTA, 2 warps per head.\n\n    grad_out and v cached in shared memory. grad_w accumulates in registers.\n    Cross-warp dldg reduction via shared memory.\n    \"\"\"\n    assert hc_mult == 4\n    num_tokens = T.dynamic('num_tokens')\n    warp_size = 32\n    warps_per_head = 2\n    num_warps = hc_mult * warps_per_head\n    threads = warp_size * num_warps\n    threads_per_head = warp_size * warps_per_head\n    assert hidden_size % threads == 0\n    elems_per_thread = hidden_size // threads\n    elems_per_warp_pair = hidden_size // threads_per_head\n    go_vec_size = 8\n    x_vec_size = 4\n\n    # NOTE Performance only tuned for hidden_size in {4096, 7168}\n    def _choose_v_vec_size(elems_per_thread):\n        for vec in [4, 2, 1]:\n            if elems_per_thread % vec == 0:\n                return vec\n\n    def _choose_go_blk_d(hidden_size, go_tile):\n        \"\"\"Largest multiple of go_tile that divides hidden_size, with >= 2 tiles.\"\"\"\n        result = go_tile\n        for blk in range(go_tile, hidden_size // 2 + 1, go_tile):\n            if hidden_size % blk == 0:\n                result = blk\n        return result\n\n    def _choose_x_blk_d(hidden_size, x_tile, hc_mult, warps_per_head):\n        \"\"\"Largest multiple of x_tile that divides hidden_size, <= hidden_size // 2, fits in smem.\"\"\"\n        smem_fixed = (hc_mult + 1) * hidden_size * 2 + hc_mult * warps_per_head * 4\n        smem_per_x = 2 * hc_mult * (2 + 2 + 4)\n        x_smem_limit = (get_max_smem_per_sm() - smem_fixed) // smem_per_x\n        x_limit = min(x_smem_limit, hidden_size // 2)\n        result = x_tile\n        for blk in range(x_tile, x_limit + 1, x_tile):\n            if hidden_size % blk == 0:\n                result = blk\n        return result\n\n    v_vec_size = _choose_v_vec_size(elems_per_thread)\n    go_blk_d = _choose_go_blk_d(hidden_size, threads_per_head * go_vec_size)\n    x_blk_d = _choose_x_blk_d(hidden_size, threads_per_head * x_vec_size, hc_mult, warps_per_head)\n\n    assert hidden_size % go_blk_d == 0 and hidden_size % x_blk_d == 0\n    assert go_blk_d % (threads_per_head * go_vec_size) == 0\n    assert x_blk_d % (threads_per_head * x_vec_size) == 0\n    assert go_blk_d + x_blk_d <= hidden_size\n\n    def smem_layout(i, j, vs):\n        thread_id = i * threads_per_head + (j // vs) % threads_per_head\n        local_id = (j % vs) + (j // (threads_per_head * vs)) * vs\n        return thread_id, local_id\n\n    @T.prim_func\n    def engram_gate_bwd_kernel(\n        grad_out: T.Tensor[(num_tokens, hc_mult, hidden_size), T.bfloat16],\n        hidden_states: T.Tensor[(num_tokens, hc_mult, hidden_size), T.bfloat16],\n        k: T.StridedTensor[(num_tokens, hc_mult, hidden_size), (k_stride_s, k_stride_h, 1), T.bfloat16],\n        v: T.StridedTensor[(num_tokens, hidden_size), (v_stride_s, 1), T.bfloat16],\n        weight_fused: T.Tensor[(hc_mult, hidden_size), T.float],\n        dot_in: T.Tensor[(num_tokens, hc_mult), T.float],\n        gate_in: T.Tensor[(num_tokens, hc_mult), T.float],\n        rstd_x_in: T.Tensor[(num_tokens, hc_mult), T.float],\n        rstd_k_in: T.Tensor[(num_tokens, hc_mult), T.float],\n        grad_x: T.Tensor[(num_tokens, hc_mult, hidden_size), T.bfloat16],\n        grad_k: T.Tensor[(num_tokens, hc_mult, hidden_size), T.bfloat16],\n        grad_v: T.Tensor[(num_tokens, hidden_size), T.bfloat16],\n        grad_w_partial: T.Tensor[(num_persistent_blocks, hc_mult, hidden_size), T.float],\n    ):\n        with T.Kernel(num_persistent_blocks, threads=threads) as pid_p:\n            tid = T.get_thread_binding()\n            warp_id = T.get_warp_idx()\n            lane_id = T.get_lane_idx()\n            head_id = warp_id // warps_per_head\n            sub_warp_id = warp_id % warps_per_head\n\n            go_local = T.alloc_local((go_vec_size,), T.float)\n            v_local = T.alloc_local((go_vec_size,), T.float)\n            go_v_local = T.alloc_local((v_vec_size,), T.float)\n            go_x_local = T.alloc_local((x_vec_size,), T.float)\n            x_local = T.alloc_local((x_vec_size,), T.float)\n            k_local = T.alloc_local((x_vec_size,), T.float)\n            w_fused_local = T.alloc_local((x_vec_size,), T.float)\n            grad_v_partial = T.alloc_local((v_vec_size,), T.float)\n            grad_w_local = T.alloc_local((elems_per_warp_pair,), T.float)\n\n            dldg_local = T.alloc_local((1,), T.float)\n            dldg_r = T.alloc_local((1,), T.float)\n\n            gate_local = T.alloc_local((hc_mult,), T.float)\n            gate_local_hc = T.alloc_var(T.float)\n            rstd_x_local = T.alloc_var(T.float)\n            rstd_k_local = T.alloc_var(T.float)\n            dot_in_local = T.alloc_var(T.float)\n            dot_x_local = T.alloc_var(T.float)\n            dot_k_local = T.alloc_var(T.float)\n\n            go_copy_layout = T.Fragment((hc_mult, go_blk_d), forward_fn=partial(smem_layout, vs=go_vec_size))\n            x_copy_layout = T.Fragment((hc_mult, x_blk_d), forward_fn=partial(smem_layout, vs=x_vec_size))\n\n            go_smem = T.alloc_shared((hc_mult, hidden_size), T.bfloat16)\n            v_smem = T.alloc_shared((hidden_size,), T.bfloat16)\n            x_smem = T.alloc_shared((2, hc_mult, x_blk_d), T.bfloat16)\n            k_smem = T.alloc_shared((2, hc_mult, x_blk_d), T.bfloat16)\n            w_smem = T.alloc_shared((2, hc_mult, x_blk_d), T.float)\n            dldg_smem = T.alloc_shared((hc_mult, warps_per_head), T.float)\n\n            per_block = T.ceildiv(num_tokens, num_persistent_blocks)\n            t_start = T.min(per_block * pid_p, num_tokens)\n            t_end = T.min(per_block * (pid_p + 1), num_tokens)\n\n            T.clear(grad_w_local)\n\n            for i_s in T.serial(t_start, t_end):\n                # === Prologue: load grad_out and v into smem ===\n                if i_s == t_start:\n                    T.async_copy(v[i_s, :], v_smem)\n                    T.async_copy(grad_out[i_s, :, :go_blk_d], go_smem[:, :go_blk_d], loop_layout=go_copy_layout)\n                    T.ptx_wait_group(1)\n                    # ensure v_smem is readable by all threads\n                    T.sync_threads()\n\n                T.copy(gate_in[i_s, :], gate_local)\n\n                # Per-head scalar loads\n                gate_local_hc = gate_in[i_s, head_id]\n                rstd_x_local = rstd_x_in[i_s, head_id]\n                rstd_k_local = rstd_k_in[i_s, head_id]\n                dot_in_local = dot_in[i_s, head_id]\n\n                T.clear(dldg_local)\n\n                go_sub_blks = go_blk_d // (threads_per_head * go_vec_size)\n                num_go_tiles = hidden_size // go_blk_d\n\n                # === Pass 1a: dldg — two warps per head ===\n                for i_b in T.serial(1, num_go_tiles):\n                    T.async_copy(grad_out[i_s, :, i_b * go_blk_d:(i_b + 1) * go_blk_d],\n                                 go_smem[:, i_b * go_blk_d:(i_b + 1) * go_blk_d],\n                                 loop_layout=go_copy_layout)\n                    T.ptx_wait_group(1)\n                    for i_sub in T.serial(go_sub_blks):\n                        go_base = (i_b - 1) * go_blk_d + i_sub * threads_per_head * go_vec_size + sub_warp_id * warp_size * go_vec_size\n                        for i_k in T.vectorized(go_vec_size):\n                            go_local[i_k] = go_smem[head_id, go_base + lane_id * go_vec_size + i_k]\n                            v_local[i_k] = v_smem[go_base + lane_id * go_vec_size + i_k]\n                        for i_k in T.serial(go_vec_size):\n                            dldg_local[0] += go_local[i_k] * v_local[i_k]\n\n                # Epilogue: process last go tile\n                T.ptx_wait_group(0)\n                for i_sub in T.serial(go_sub_blks):\n                    go_base = (num_go_tiles - 1) * go_blk_d + i_sub * threads_per_head * go_vec_size + sub_warp_id * warp_size * go_vec_size\n                    for i_k in T.vectorized(go_vec_size):\n                        go_local[i_k] = go_smem[head_id, go_base + lane_id * go_vec_size + i_k]\n                        v_local[i_k] = v_smem[go_base + lane_id * go_vec_size + i_k]\n                    for i_k in T.serial(go_vec_size):\n                        dldg_local[0] += go_local[i_k] * v_local[i_k]\n\n                # Cross-warp dldg reduction via smem\n                dldg_local[0] = T.warp_reduce_sum(dldg_local[0])\n                if lane_id == 0:\n                    dldg_smem[head_id, sub_warp_id] = dldg_local[0]\n                T.sync_threads()\n\n                # Prefetch next token's v\n                if i_s + 1 < t_end:\n                    T.async_copy(v[i_s + 1, :], v_smem)\n\n                T.async_copy(hidden_states[i_s, :, :x_blk_d], x_smem[0, :, :], loop_layout=x_copy_layout)\n                T.async_copy(k[i_s, :, :x_blk_d], k_smem[0, :, :], loop_layout=x_copy_layout)\n                T.async_copy(weight_fused[:, :x_blk_d], w_smem[0, :, :], loop_layout=x_copy_layout)\n\n                # Gate derivative\n                dldg_r[0] = dldg_smem[head_id, 0] + dldg_smem[head_id, 1]\n                dldg_r[0] = T.Select(\n                    T.abs(dot_in_local) * scalar * rstd_x_local * rstd_k_local < clamp_value,\n                    0.0,\n                    dldg_r[0] * gate_local_hc * (1.0 - gate_local_hc) * 0.5 * T.sqrt(scalar * rstd_x_local * rstd_k_local / T.abs(dot_in_local))\n                )\n\n                # === Pass 1b: grad_v ===\n                for i in T.serial(elems_per_thread // v_vec_size):\n                    T.clear(grad_v_partial)\n                    for i_h in T.unroll(hc_mult):\n                        for i_k in T.vectorized(v_vec_size):\n                            go_v_local[i_k] = go_smem[i_h, i * threads * v_vec_size + tid * v_vec_size + i_k]\n                        for i_k in T.vectorized(v_vec_size):\n                            grad_v_partial[i_k] += go_v_local[i_k] * gate_local[i_h]\n                    for i_k in T.vectorized(v_vec_size):\n                        grad_v[i_s, i * threads * v_vec_size + tid * v_vec_size + i_k] = grad_v_partial[i_k]\n\n                dot_x_local = dot_in_local * rstd_x_local * rstd_x_local / hidden_size\n                dot_k_local = dot_in_local * rstd_k_local * rstd_k_local / hidden_size\n\n                # === Pass 2: grad_x, grad_k, grad_w — pipelined x/k, 2 warps per head ===\n                x_sub_blks = x_blk_d // (threads_per_head * x_vec_size)\n                num_x_tiles = hidden_size // x_blk_d\n\n                for i_b in T.unroll(1, num_x_tiles):\n                    phase = i_b % 2\n                    prev = (i_b - 1) % 2\n\n                    T.async_copy(hidden_states[i_s, :, i_b * x_blk_d:(i_b + 1) * x_blk_d],\n                                 x_smem[phase, :, :], loop_layout=x_copy_layout)\n                    T.async_copy(k[i_s, :, i_b * x_blk_d:(i_b + 1) * x_blk_d],\n                                 k_smem[phase, :, :], loop_layout=x_copy_layout)\n                    T.async_copy(weight_fused[:, i_b * x_blk_d:(i_b + 1) * x_blk_d],\n                                 w_smem[phase, :, :], loop_layout=x_copy_layout)\n\n                    T.ptx_wait_group(3)\n\n                    for i_sub in T.unroll(x_sub_blks):\n                        sub_off = i_sub * (threads_per_head * x_vec_size) + sub_warp_id * (warp_size * x_vec_size)\n                        global_base = (i_b - 1) * x_blk_d + sub_off\n                        reg_base = ((i_b - 1) * x_sub_blks + i_sub) * x_vec_size\n                        for i_k in T.vectorized(x_vec_size):\n                            go_x_local[i_k] = go_smem[head_id, global_base + lane_id * x_vec_size + i_k]\n                            x_local[i_k] = x_smem[prev, head_id, sub_off + lane_id * x_vec_size + i_k]\n                            k_local[i_k] = k_smem[prev, head_id, sub_off + lane_id * x_vec_size + i_k]\n                            w_fused_local[i_k] = w_smem[prev, head_id, sub_off + lane_id * x_vec_size + i_k]\n                        for i_k in T.vectorized(x_vec_size):\n                            grad_x[i_s, head_id, global_base + lane_id * x_vec_size + i_k] = \\\n                                go_x_local[i_k] + dldg_r[0] * (k_local[i_k] * w_fused_local[i_k] - x_local[i_k] * dot_x_local)\n                            grad_k[i_s, head_id, global_base + lane_id * x_vec_size + i_k] = \\\n                                dldg_r[0] * (x_local[i_k] * w_fused_local[i_k] - k_local[i_k] * dot_k_local)\n                        for i_k in T.serial(x_vec_size):\n                            grad_w_local[reg_base + i_k] += dldg_r[0] * x_local[i_k] * k_local[i_k]\n\n                # Epilogue: process last x/k/w tile + prefetch next token's go\n                T.ptx_wait_group(0)\n\n                # ensure v_smem is ready and go_smem[:go_blk_d] is clean\n                T.sync_threads()\n                if i_s + 1 < t_end:\n                    T.async_copy(grad_out[i_s + 1, :, :go_blk_d], go_smem[:, :go_blk_d], loop_layout=go_copy_layout)\n\n                for i_sub in T.unroll(x_sub_blks):\n                    sub_off = i_sub * (threads_per_head * x_vec_size) + sub_warp_id * (warp_size * x_vec_size)\n / hidden_size + eps)\n    rstd_k = 1.0 / tl.sqrt(sum_k2 / hidden_size + eps)\n    \n    scaled_dot = sum_xkw * rstd_x * rstd_k * scalar\n    abs_dot = tl.abs(scaled_dot)\n    sqrt_dot = So most v loads will go to HBM.\n\nWait actually, the order of execution matters. If 4 CTAs for one token run concurrently on the same SM (or nearby SMs), they share L2. The L2 hit rate for v would be high. But L2 is shared across all SMs, so the 4MB L2 only helps a few hundred tokens at a time.\n\nOK let me just try both approaches. Start with simple, see what we get, then optimize.\n\nLet me also think about the persistent CTA approach. Each CTA processes a contiguous chunk of (token, head) pairs. For example, each CTA does 32 (token, head) pairs. Then the CTA loads weight_fused only once (saved across iterations). But weight_fused is only 64KB and gets cached in L2 anyway, so this is marginal.\n\nThe bigger benefit of persistent: amortization of the v load. If a CTA processes all 4 heads of one token, v[t] is loaded once. But this is what I described above (CTA per token with 4 heads looped inside).\n\nLet me think about an even simpler optimization: instead of one CTA per (token, head), use one CTA per (token, head_block) where head_block could be 1 or 4. For head_block=4, the CTA loads v once.\n\nI'll start with the simple approach and benchmark.\n\nLet me write the code now.\n\n```python\nimport torch\nimport triton\nimport triton.language as tl\n\n\n@triton.jit\ndef engram_gate_fwd_kernel(\n    x_ptr, k_ptr, v_ptr, w_ptr,\n    out_ptr, dot_ptr, gate_ptr, rstd_x_ptr, rstd_k_ptr,\n    hc_mult: tl.constexpr,\n    hidden_size,\n    inv_hidden_size,\n    eps,\n    clamp_value,\n    scalar,\n    save_for_backward: tl.constexpr,\n    BLOCK_SIZE: tl.constexpr,\n):\n    pid = tl.program_id(0)\n    token = pid // hc_mult\n    head = pid % hc_mult\n    \n    base = token * hc_mult * hidden_size + head * hidden_size\n    \n    offs = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_SIZE)\n    mask = offs < hidden_size\n    \n    x = tl.load(x_ptr + base + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)\n    k = tl.load(k_ptr + base + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)\n    w = tl.load(w_ptr + head * hidden_size + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0)\n    v = tl.load(v_ptr + token * hidden_size + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)\n    \n    sum_x2 = tl.sum(x * x)\n    sum_k2 = tl.sum(k * k)\n    sum_xkw = tl.sum(x * k * w)\n    \n    rstd_x = 1.0 / tl.sqrt(sum_x2 * inv_hidden_size + eps)\n    rstd_k = 1.0 / tl.sqrt(sum_k2 * inv_hidden_size + eps)\n    \n    scaled_dot = sum_xkw * rstd_x * rstd_k * scalar\n    abs_dot = tl.abs(scaled_dot)\n    sqrt_dot = tl.sqrt(tl.maximum(abs_dot, clamp_value))\n    sign_dot = tl.where(scaled_dot >= 0.0, 1.0, -1.0)\n    gate_score = tl.sigmoid(sign_dot * sqrt_dot)\n    \n    out = x + gate_score * v\n    tl.store(out_ptr + base + offs, out.to(tl.bfloat16), mask=mask)\n    \n    if save_for_backward:\n        tl.store(dot_ptr + token * hc_mult + head, sum_xkw)\n        tl.store(gate_ptr + token * hc_mult + head, gate_score)\n        tl.store(rstd_x_ptr + token * hc_mult + head, rstd_x)\n        tl.store(rstd_k_ptr + token * hc_mult + head, rstd_k)\n\n\ndef engram_gate_fwd_triton(\n    hidden_states: torch.Tensor,\n    k: torch.Tensor,\n    v: torch.Tensor,\n    weight_fused: torch.Tensor,\n    eps: float,\n    clamp_value: float,\n    save_for_backward: bool = True,\n):\n    num_tokens, hc_mult, hidden_size = hidden_states.shape\n    scalar = hidden_size ** -0.5\n    \n    output = torch.empty_like(hidden_states)\n    \n    if save_for_backward:\n        dot = torch.empty((num_tokens, hc_mult), dtype=torch.float32, device=hidden_states.device)\n        gate_score = torch.empty((num_tokens, hc_mult), dtype=torch.float32, device=hidden_states.device)\n        rstd_x = torch.empty((num_tokens, hc_mult), dtype=torch.float32, device=hidden_states.device)\n        rstd_k = torch.empty((num_tokens, hc_mult), dtype=torch.float32, device=hidden_states.device)\n    else:\n        dot = gate_score = rstd_x = rstd_k = None\n    \n    BLOCK_SIZE = triton.next_power_of_2(hidden_size)\n    grid = (num_tokens * hc_mult,)\n    \n    engram_gate_fwd_kernel[grid](\n        hidden_states, k, v, weight_fused,\n        output, dot, gate_score, rstd_x, rstd_k,\n        hc_mult=hc_mult,\n        hidden_size=hidden_size,\n        inv_hidden_size=1.0 / hidden_size,\n        eps=eps,\n        clamp_value=clamp_value,\n        scalar=scalar,\n        save_for_backward=save_for_backward,\n        BLOCK_SIZE=BLOCK_SIZE,\n    )\n    \n    return output, dot, gate_score, rstd_x, rstd_k\n```\n\nWait, I think for hidden_size not power of 2, masking is fine. The product is computed in fp32. The weight_fused = wh.float() * we.float() (so fp32 product). So `sum(x * w_fused * k)` is mathematically identical (just reordered).\n\nBut the floating-point order matters! `x * (wh * we) * k` vs `(x * wh) * (we * k)` give slightly different results.\n\nReference: `raw_dot = einsum('...d,...d->...', x * wh, k_f * we)`. So this is `sum_i (x_i * wh_i) * (k_i * we_i)`. The product `x * wh` is bf16*fp32 → fp32 (auto-promoted), then `k_f * we` similarly, then multiply: fp32*fp32 → fp32.\n\nMy code: `sum(x * k * w)` where x,k are bf16→fp32 and w is fp32 weight_fused. So `(x * k)` is fp32*fp32 → fp32, then * w (fp32) → fp32. \n\nThese are different floating-point orderings! Let me check:\n\nReference: a*b*c*d where a=x, b=wh, c=k, d=we. Computed as (a*b)*(c*d).\nMy code: a*c*(b*d) where b*d = w. Computed as a*c*w = (a*c)*w.\n\nHmm. These are different. Is the difference smaller than that?\n\nActually for random bf16 values, x_i, wh_i, k_i, we_i are all ~O(1) magnitude. Products are O(1). Sums of 4096 O(1) values are O(64) magnitude. For sum of 4096 values each ~1, the sum is ~64, ULP(64) ≈ 2^{-17} ≈ 7.6e-6. So accumulated error ~ N * ULP * max_term ~ 4096 * 7.6e-6 * 1 = 0.03 absolute.\n\nHmm, but that's an extremely conservative bound. The actual error is much smaller because of cancellation.\n\nIn practice, for sums of random values, the accumulated error is O(sqrt(N) * ULP * sum_abs) which is much smaller.\n\nFor the cosine similarity, we need 1 - sim < 2e-10. If x and y differ by absolute error ε_abs and have magnitude M, then relative error is ε_abs/M. calc_diff ≈ (ε_abs/M)² / 2.\n\nIf ε_abs ≈ 1e-3 (random drift) and M ≈ 64, then calc_diff ≈ (1e-3/64)² / 2 ≈ 1.2e-10. With 4MB L2 and 8KB per v token, ~500 tokens worth of v fit in L2. Sequential access of tokens means good L2 hit rate.\n\nActually, on second thought, the L2 hit rate depends on access pattern. If we process tokens in order, the v for the current token is loaded by head 0 first (CTA-0), then head 1 (CTA-1) etc. If all 4 CTAs for one token are scheduled close together, the second through fourth heads hit L2.\n\nBut scheduling order isn't guaranteed. CTAs are scheduled to SMs in pid order. With grid = (num_tokens * hc_mult,), the first 256 CTAs go to 256 SMs. Then next 256. So CTAs (0, 1, 2, 3) for token 0 are scheduled to SMs 0, 1, 2, 3. They run in parallel (or near-parallel), all reading v[0]. The first one loads from HBM, the others hit L2.\n\nHmm but with 32768 CTAs and 256 SMs, each SM runs 128 CTAs sequentially (or in waves). Let me just try the simple approach first.\n\nOption B: CTA per token, loop over 4 heads inside. Each CTA loads v once. Process:\n```\nload v (8KB)\nfor h in 0..3:\n    load x[t, h], k[t, h], w[h]\n    compute reductions\n    compute gate_score[h]\nfor h in 0..3:\n    out[t, h] = x[t, h] + gate_score[h] * v  # recompute x? or save it\n    store out[t, h]\n```\n\nIssue: we need x in registers for the output stage. If we process heads sequentially, we need to either:\n(a) keep all 4 x's in registers (4 * 4096 * 4 = 64KB per CTA = too much)\n(b) reload x for output stage\n\nIf we reload x, total x reads = 256MB * 2 = 512MB. Worse than Option A (256MB).\n\nSo Option B isn't better.\n\nOption C: Two-pass approach. Pass 1: compute reductions and gate scores. Pass 2: compute output.\n- Pass 1: read x, k, w → write gate_score (small)\n- Pass 2: read x, v → write out\n\nTotal x reads: 512MB. Worse.\n\nOption D: CTA per (token, head) but use a separate kernel for v loading. Doesn't make sense.\n\nOption E: One kernel, one CTA per (token, head) but process multiple heads per CTA. E.g., each CTA does (token_block, head_block) where head_block=4. Then v is loaded once per token_block.\n\nFor each CTA:\n- Load x[t, 0:4, :], k[t, 0:4, :], v[t, :], w[0:4, :]\n- BLOCK_SIZE = hidden_size, num heads in CTA = 4\n- Total elements: 4*4096 = 16384 for x/k/v per token\n\nThis is too big for registers.\n\nOption F: Persistent CTA approach. Each CTA is assigned a range of (token, head) pairs. For consecutive heads of the same token, v is shared.\n\nIf a CTA processes (token, head=0), (token, head=1), ..., (token, head=3), then v[t] is loaded once.\n\n```\nfor token in assigned_tokens:\n    v = load v[token]\n    for head in 0..3:\n        x = load x[token, head]\n        k = load k[token, head]\n        w = load w[head]\n        compute reductions\n        compute gate\n        out = x + gate * v\n        store out[token, head]\n```\n\nTotal reads: x=256MB, k=256MB, v=64MB, w=64KB. Total writes: 256MB. Grand total: 832MB.\n\nThis is 19% less bandwidth than Option A. At 4 TB/s, 208μs vs 256μs.\n\nNow, the CTA does 4x more work, so we have 1/4 the CTAs = 8192. With 256 SMs, that's 32 CTAs per SM. Each CTA does 4 token-head pairs sequentially. Inside the CTA, the inner head loop has no inter-iteration dependency (different memory regions).\n\nWait actually we could parallelize the heads within the CTA. But Triton blocks are typically for SIMT-style work. The simpler approach is to have a CTA process one (token, head) pair but iterate over multiple in sequence.\n\nActually for the persistent kernel, the simplest is:\n- Each CTA processes N consecutive (token, head) pairs\n- For efficiency, group them by token to share v loads\n\nIf N = 4 and we group by head (token, head=0..3, then next token), v is loaded once per 4 iterations.\n\nLet me design this:\n\n```python\n@triton.jit\ndef kernel(x_ptr, k_ptr, v_ptr, w_ptr, ...):\n    pid = tl.program_id(0)  # CTA id\n    # Each CTA processes a chunk of (token, head) pairs\n    # Group by token: 4 consecutive pids share a token\n    TOKENS_PER_CTA = 1  # process 1 token (with 4 heads)\n    \n    num_tokens = ...\n    num_ctas = num_tokens  # one CTA per token\n    \n    token = pid\n    if token >= num_tokens:\n        return\n    \n    v = tl.load(v_ptr + token * hidden_size + offs, mask=mask)\n    \n    for head in range(hc_mult):  # hc_mult=4\n        x = tl.load(x_ptr + token * hc_mult * hidden_size + head * hidden_size + offs, ...)\n        k = tl.load(k_ptr + ...)\n        w = tl.load(w_ptr + head * hidden_size + offs, ...)\n        \n        sum_x2 = tl.sum(x*x)\n        sum_k2 = tl.sum(k*k)\n        sum_xkw = tl.sum(x*w*k)\n        rstd_x = 1.0 / tl.sqrt(sum_x2 * inv_h + eps)\n        rstd_k = 1.0 / tl.sqrt(sum_k2 * inv_h + eps)\n        scaled_dot = sum_xkw * rstd_x * rstd_k * scalar\n        abs_dot = tl.abs(scaled_dot)\n        sqrt_dot = tl.sqrt(tl.maximum(abs_dot, clamp_value))\n        sign_dot = tl.where(scaled_dot >= 0.0, 1.0, -1.0)\n        gate_score = tl.sigmoid(sign_dot * sqrt_dot)\n        \n        out = x + gate_score * v\n        tl.store(out_ptr + ..., out.to(tl.bfloat16), mask=mask)\n        \n        if save_for_backward:\n            tl.store(dot_ptr + token * hc_mult + head, sum_xkw)\n            tl.store(gate_ptr + token * hc_mult + head, gate_score)\n            tl.store(rstd_x_ptr + token * hc_mult + head, rstd_x)\n            tl.store(rstd_k_ptr + token * hc_mult + head, rstd_k)\n```\n\nIssues with this approach:\n- Per-CTA work is 4x bigger: instead of processing 1 (token, head), process 4.\n- Grid is num_tokens = 8192. With 256 SMs, 32 CTAs per SM. Fine.\n- But each CTA is heavier (loads more memory, does more compute).\n- Register pressure: x, k, w are re-loaded each head iteration (good, frees registers). v is kept across iterations.\n- Total per-CTA fp32 in registers at any time: x + k + w + v = 4 * 4096 * 4 = 64KB. With num_warps=8 (256 threads), 256 bytes per thread = 64 regs. OK.\n\nActually wait, this approach doesn't keep x and k loaded across head iterations. Within ONE head iteration, x and k are both live. With 4 heads iterated, x is overwritten each iteration (or held in registers).\n\nActually the simpler interpretation: in each head iteration, the CTA loads x, k, w fresh, computes gate_score, then computes out = x + gate_score * v using the v it already loaded. x is only live for one head iteration. So peak registers are x + k + w + v ≈ 64KB per CTA = 256B/thread with 8 warps.\n\nHmm but x, k, w, v are each 4096 elements * 4 bytes = 16KB. Total 64KB. With num_warps=8, 256 threads, each thread has 4 elements per array * 4 bytes = 16 bytes per array * 4 arrays = 64 bytes. With gate_score in registers too, maybe 80 bytes. About 20 regs. Very comfortable.\n\nOK let me write this. I think this is the right approach.\n\nWait, but does the kernel allow efficient reduction with this? Let's see. tl.sum reduces across the BLOCK_SIZE dimension. With BLOCK_SIZE=4096 and num_warps=8, that's 4096 elements summed.\n\nEach thread has 16 elements (after broadcasting from register arrays). tl.sum does the warp + cross-warp reduction. Should be efficient.\n\nAlright let me write the code.\n\nActually wait, I realize there's a subtlety with Triton. When I write:\n```python\nv = tl.load(v_ptr + token * hidden_size + offs, mask=mask)\nfor head in range(hc_mult):\n    x = tl.load(x_ptr + ...)\n    ...\n```\n\nThe for loop is at the kernel level. The grid is 8192 CTAs instead of 32768. With 256 SMs, that's still plenty of parallelism (32 CTAs/SM).\n\nLet me write the persistent version (1 CTA per token) first.\n\n```python\n@triton.jit\ndef engram_gate_fwd_kernel(\n    x_ptr, k_ptr, v_ptr, w_ptr,\n    out_ptr, dot_ptr, gate_ptr, rstd_x_ptr, rstd_k_ptr,\n    hc_mult: tl.constexpr,\n    hidden_size,\n    inv_hidden_size,\n    eps,\n    clamp_value,\n    scalar,\n    save_for_backward: tl.constexpr,\n    BLOCK_SIZE: tl.constexpr,\n):\n    pid = tl.program_id(0)\n    \n    offs = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_SIZE)\n    mask = offs < hidden_size\n    \n    token = pid\n    v_off = v_ptr + token * hidden_size\n    v = tl.load(v_off + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)\n    \n    for head in tl.static_range(hc_mult):\n        xk_base = x_ptr + token * hc_mult * hidden_size + head * hidden_size\n        x = tl.load(xk_base + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)\n        k = tl.load(xk_base + offs + (k_ptr - x_ptr), mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)\n        w = tl.load(w_ptr + head * hidden_size + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0)\n        \n        sum_x2 = tl.sum(x * x)\n        sum_k2 = tl.sum(k * k)\n        sum_xkw = tl.sum(x * w * k)\n        \n        rstd_x = 1.0 / tl.sqrt(sum_x2 * inv_hidden_size + eps)\n        rstd_k = 1.0 / tl.sqrt(sum_k2 * inv_hidden_size + eps)\n        \n        scaled_dot = sum_xkw * rstd_x * rstd_k * scalar\n        abs_dot = tl.abs(scaled_dot)\n        sqrt_dot = tl.sqrt(tl.maximum(abs_dot, clamp_value))\n        sign_dot = tl.where(scaled_dot >= 0.0, 1.0, -1.0)\n        gate_score = tl.sigmoid(sign_dot * sqrt_dot)\n        \n        out = x + gate_score * v\n        tl.store(xk_base + offs + (out_ptr - x_ptr), out.to(tl.bfloat16), mask=mask)\n        \n        if save_for_backward:\n            base_idx = token * hc_mult + head\n            tl.store(dot_ptr + base_idx, sum_xkw)\n            tl.store(gate_ptr + base_idx, gate_score)\n            tl.store(rstd_x_ptr + base_idx, rstd_x)\n            tl.store(rstd_k_ptr + base_idx, rstd_k)\n```\n\nWait this is getting messy with the pointer arithmetic. Let me clean up.\n\nActually using offsets is simpler:\n```python\n@triton.jit\ndef kernel(\n    x_ptr, k_ptr, v_ptr, w_ptr,\n    out_ptr, dot_ptr, gate_ptr, rstd_x_ptr, rstd_k_ptr,\n    token_stride_x, head_stride_x,  # x strides\n    hc_mult: tl.constexpr,\n    hidden_size,\n    inv_hidden_size,\n    eps,\n    clamp_value,\n    scalar,\n    save_for_backward: tl.constexpr,\n    BLOCK_SIZE: tl.constexpr,\n):\n    pid = tl.program_id(0)\n    token = pid\n    \n    offs = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_SIZE)\n    mask = offs < hidden_size\n    \n    v = tl.load(v_ptr + token * hidden_size + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)\n    \n    for head in tl.static_range(hc_mult):\n        x_off = token * token_stride_x + head * head_stride_x\n        x = tl.load(x_ptr + x_off + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)\n        k = tl.load(k_ptr + x_off + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)\n        w = tl.load(w_ptr + head * hidden_size + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0)\n        \n        sum_x2 = tl.sum(x * x)\n        sum_k2 = tl.sum(k * k)\n        sum_xkw = tl.sum(x * w * k)\n        \n        rstd_x = 1.0 / tl.sqrt(sum_x2 * inv_hidden_size + eps)\n        rstd_k = 1.0 / tl.sqrt(sum_k2 * inv_hidden_size + eps)\n        \n        scaled_dot = sum_xkw * rstd_x * rstd_k * scalar\n        abs_dot = tl.abs(scaled_dot)\n        sqrt_dot = tl.sqrt(tl.maximum(abs_dot, clamp_value))\n        sign_dot = tl.where(scaled_dot >= 0.0, 1.0, -1.0)\n        gate_score = tl.sigmoid(sign_dot * sqrt_dot)\n        \n        out = x + gate_score * v\n        tl.store(out_ptr + x_off + offs, out.to(tl.bfloat16), mask=mask)\n        \n        if save_for_backward:\n            base_idx = token * hc_mult + head\n            tl.store(dot_ptr + base_idx, sum_xkw)\n            tl.store(gate_ptr + base_idx, gate_score)\n            tl.store(rstd_x_ptr + base_idx, rstd_x)\n            tl.store(rstd_k_ptr + base_idx, rstd_k)\n```\n\nOK let me actually try this. triton.language as tl\n\n\n@triton.jit\ndef engram_gate_fwd_kernel(\n    x_ptr, k_ptr, v_ptr, w_ptr,\n    out_ptr,\n    dot_ptr, gate_ptr, rstd_x_ptr, rstd_k_ptr,\n    hc_mult: tl.constexpr,\n    hidden_size: tl.constexpr,\n    token_stride_x: tl.constexpr,\n    head_stride_x: tl.constexpr,\n    inv_h,\n    eps,\n    clamp_value,\n    scalar,\n    save_for_backward: tl.constexpr,\n    BLOCK_SIZE: tl.constexpr,\n):\n    pid = tl.program_id(0)\n    token = pid\n    \n    offs = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_SIZE)\n    mask = offs < hidden_size\n    \n    # Load v once, share across heads\n    v hidden_size + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0)\n        \n        sum_x2 = tl.sum(x * x)\n        sum_k2 = tl.sum(k * k)\n        sum_xkw = tl.sum(x * w * k)\n        \n        rstd_x = tl.rsqrt(sum_x2 * engram_gate_fwd_triton(\n    hidden_states, k, v, weight_fused,\n    eps, clamp_value, save_for_backward=True,\n):\n    num_tokens, hc_mult, hidden_size = hidden_states.shape\n    scalar = hidden_size ** -0.5\n    \n    output = torch.empty_like(hidden_states)\n    \n    if save_for_backward:\n        dot = torch.empty((num_tokens, hc_mult), dtype=torch.float32, device=hidden_states.device)\n        gate_score = torch.empty((num_tokens, hc_mult), dtype=torch.float32, device=hidden_states.device)\n        rstd_x = torch.empty((num_tokens, hc_mult), dtype=torch.float32, device=hidden_states.device)\n        rstd_k = torch.empty((num_tokens, hc_mult), dtype=torch.float32, device=hidden_states.device)\n    else:\n        dot = gate_score = rstd_x = rstd_k = None\n    \n    BLOCK_SIZE = triton.next_power_of_2(hidden_size)\n    grid = (num_tokens,)\n    \n    engram_gate_fwd_kernel[grid](\n        hidden_states, k, v, weight_fused,\n        output, dot, gate_score, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)\n    k = tl.load(k_ptr + x_off + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)\n    w = tl.load(w_ptr + head * hidden_size + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0)\n    v = tl.load(v_ptr + token * hidden_size + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)\n\n    sum_x2 = tl.sum(x * x)\n    sum_k2 = tl.sum(k * k)\n    sum_xkw = tl.sum(x * w * k)\n\n    rstd_x = tl.rsqrt(sum_x2 * inv_h + eps)\n    rstd_k = tl.rsqrt(sum_k2 * inv_h + eps)\n\n    scaled_dot = sum_xkw * rstd_x * rstd_k * scalar\n    abs_dot = tl.abs(scaled_dot)\n    sqrt_dot = tl.sqrt(tl.maximum(abs_dot, clamp_value))\n    sign_dot = tl.where(scaled_dot >= 0.0, 1.0, -1.0)\n    gate_score = tl.sigmoid(sign_dot * sqrt_dot)\n\n    out = x + gate_score * v\n    tl.store(out_ptr + x_off + offs, out.to(tl.bfloat16), mask=mask)\n\n    if save_for_backward:\n        base_idx = token * hc_mult + head\n        tl.store(dot_ptr + base_idx, sum_xkw)\n        tl.store(gate_ptr + base_idx, gate_score)\n        tl.store(rstd_x_ptr + base_idx, rstd_x)\n        tl.store(rstd_k_ptr + base_idx, rstd_k)\n\n\ndef engram_gate_fwd_triton_simple(\n    hidden_states, k, v, weight_fused,\n    eps, clamp_value, save_for_backward=True,\n    num_warps=8, num_stages=1,\n):\n    num_tokens, hc_mult, hidden_size = hidden_states.shape\n    scalar = hidden_size ** -0.5\n    output = torch.empty_like(hidden_states)\n    if save_for_backward:\n        dot = torch.empty((num_tokens, hc_mult), dtype=torch.float32, device=hidden_states.device)\n        gate_score = torch.empty((num_tokens, hc_mult), dtype=torch.float32, device=hidden_states.device)\n        rstd_x = torch.empty((num_tokens, hc_mult), dtype=torch.float32, device=hidden_states.device)\n        rstd_k = torch.empty((num_tokens, hc_mult), dtype=torch.float32, device=hidden_states.device)\n    else:\n        dot = gate_score = rstd_x = rstd_k = None\n    BLOCK_SIZE = triton.next_power_of_2(hidden_size)\n    grid = (num_tokens * hc_mult,)\n    _engram_gate_fwd_kernel_simple[grid](\n        hidden_states, k, v, weight_fused,\n        output, dot, gate_score, rstd_x, rstd_k,\n        hc_mult=hc_mult,\n        hidden_size=hidden_size,\n        inv_h=1.0 / hidden_size,\n        eps=eps,\n        clamp_value=clamp_value,\n        scalar=scalar,\n        save_for_backward=save_for_backward,\n        BLOCK_SIZE=BLOCK_SIZE,\n        num_warps=num_warps,\n        num_stages=num_stages,\n    )\n    return output, dot, gate_score, rstd_x, rstd_k\n\n\nfrom tile_kernels.engram import engram_gate_fwd\n\ntorch.manual_seed(42)\nnum_tokens = 8192\nhc_mult = 4\nhidden_size = 4096\neps = 1e-20\nclamp_value = 1e-6\n\nx = torch.randn(num_tokens, hc_mult, hidden_size, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')\nk = torch.randn(num_tokens, hc_mult, hidden_size, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')\nv = torch.randn(num_tokens, hidden_size, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')\nwh = torch.randn(hc_mult, hidden_size, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')\nwe = torch.randn(hc_mult, hidden_size, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device='cuda')\nweight_fused = wh.float() * we.float()\n\n# Reference TileLang\nfor _ in range(20):\n    _ = engram_gate_fwd(x, k, v, weight_fused, eps, clamp_value, save_for_backward=True)\ntorch.cuda.synchronize()\n\nN = 100\nstart = time.perf_counter()\nfor _ in range(N):\n    _ = engram_gate_fwd(x, k, v, weight_fused, eps, clamp_value, save_for_backward=True)\ntorch.cuda.synchronize()\ntl_time = (time.perf_counter() - start) / N * 1e6\nprint(f\"TileLang: {tl_time:.1f} us\")\n\nfor num_warps in [2, 4, 8, 16]:\n    for num_stages in They run in parallel. When they all read v[0], only the first one goes to HBM (or maybe a few do, depending on L2 latency vs CTA launch).\n\nFor 4 CTAs starting within a few microseconds, they all hit the L2 cache for v (since L2 latency is ~100ns and CTA launch is ~μs).\n\nOK so v reuse works in the simple kernel.\n\nFor the multi-token kernel with tpc=1, the first 256 CTAs are (token=0..255, head=0). They all read different v's (v[0], v[1], ..., v[255]). No v reuse. w[0] is shared though.\n\nHmm so the multi-token kernel doesn't have v reuse, but does have w reuse. The simple kernel has v reuse (via L2) and w reuse (via L2).\n\nIn both cases, all data ends up in L2 after the first few accesses. So we have 5 intra-warp levels (log2(32)) + 1 cross-warp via SMEM = 6 levels total.\n\nWith num_warps=4 (128 threads), log2(128) = 7 levels. 5 intra + 2 cross.\n\nWith num_warps=8 (256 threads), log2(256) = 8 levels. 5 intra + 3 cross.\n\nMore warps = more reduction overhead but less work per thread.\n\nThe total work per thread decreases with more warps. So the reduction overhead doesn't matter much.\n\nLet me try a completely different approach: split the hidden dimension across multiple CTAs (split-K reduction).\n\nWait that adds complexity. Let me just stick with the simple kernel.\n\nActually, let me try one more thing: combine the dot computation with the output computation more tightly. Maybe use FMA.\n\n```python\nout = x + gate_score * v\n```\n\nThis is `x + gate * v`. In fp32, this is `(gate * v) + x`. With FMA, this could be `fma(gate, v, x)`. Let me check if Triton uses FMA automatically.\n\nActually `gate_score * v + x` should be optimized to FMA by the compiler.\n\nHmm. Let me look at what optimizations are happening.\n\nActually, let me try one more experiment: compute everything in fewer ops.\n\nThe current kernel:\n1. Load x, k, w, v\n2. sum_x2 = sum(x*x)\n3. sum_k2 = sum(k*k)\n4. sum_xkw = sum(x*w*k)\n5. rstd_x = rsqrt(sum_x2/h + eps)\n6. rstd_k = rsqrt(sum_k2/h + eps)\n7. scaled_dot = sum_xkw * rstd_x * rstd_k * scalar\n8. abs_dot = abs(scaled_dot)\n9. sqrt_dot = sqrt(max(abs_dot, clamp))\n10. sign_dot = where(scaled_dot >= 0, 1, -1)\n11. gate = sigmoid(sign_dot * sqrt_dot)\n12. out = x + gate * v\n13. Store out\n\nThis is reasonably tight. Let me see if there's any redundant work.\n\nHmm, the dot product computation could be split into multiple parts to overlap with output. But that adds complexity.\n\nActually, let me try one more variant: precompute the inverse hidden size once outside the kernel.\n\nWait I already do that: `inv_h = 1.0 / hidden_size`.\n\nLet me also see if the scalar (1/sqrt(hidden_size)) could be precomputed. I already do.\n\nOK let me finalize.\n\nActually, let me also think about whether to inline the constants or pass them as args. Currently I pass eps, clamp_value, scalar, inv_h as args. Triton specializes on constexpr but not on runtime args.\n\nLet me make eps, clamp_value constexpr if possible. Actually no, they're user-provided (eps=1e-20, clamp=1e-6), so they could be either. Let me keep them as args.\n\nOK final code:\n\n```python\nimport torch\nimport triton\nimport triton.language as tl\n\n\n@triton.jit\ndef _engram_gate_fwd_kernel(\n    x_ptr, k_ptr, v_ptr, w_ptr,\n    out_ptr,\n    dot_ptr, gate_ptr, rstd_x_ptr, rstd_k_ptr,\n    hc_mult: tl.constexpr,\n    hidden_size: tl.constexpr,\n    inv_h,\n    eps,\n    clamp_value,\n    scalar,\n    save_for_backward: tl.constexpr,\n    BLOCK_SIZE: tl.constexpr,\n):\n    pid = tl.program_id(0)\n    token = pid // hc_mult\n    head = pid % hc_mult\n\n    offs = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_SIZE)\n    mask = offs < hidden_size\n\n    x_off = token * hc_mult * hidden_size + head * hidden_size\n    x = tl.load(x_ptr + x_off + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)\n    k = tl.load(k_ptr + x_off + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)\n    w = tl.load(w_ptr + head * hidden_size + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0)\n    v = tl.load(v_ptr + token * hidden_size + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)\n\n    sum_x2 = tl.sum(x * x)\n    sum_k2 = tl.sum(k * k)\n    sum_xkw = tl.sum(x * w * k)\n\n    rstd_x = tl.rsqrt(sum_x2 * inv_h + eps)\n    rstd_k = tl.rsqrt(sum_k2 * inv_h + eps)\n\n    scaled_dot = sum_xkw * rstd_x * rstd_k * scalar\n    abs_dot = tl.abs(scaled_dot)\n    sqrt_dot = tl.sqrt(tl.maximum(abs_dot, clamp_value))\n    sign_dot = tl.where(scaled_dot >= 0.0, 1.0, -1.0)\n    gate_score = tl.sigmoid(sign_dot * sqrt_dot)\n\n    out = x + gate_score * v\n    tl.store(out_ptr + x_off + offs, out.to(tl.bfloat16), mask=mask)\n\n    if save_for_backward:\n        base_idx = token * hc_mult + head\n        tl.store(dot_ptr + base_idx, sum_xkw)\n        tl.store(gate_ptr + base_idx, gate_score)\n        tl.store(rstd_x_ptr + base_idx, rstd_x)\n        tl.store(rstd_k_ptr + base_idx, rstd_k)\n\n\ndef engram_gate_fwd_triton(\n    hidden_states,\n    k,\n    v,\n    weight_fused,\n    eps,\n    clamp_value,\n    save_for_backward=True,\n):\n    num_tokens, hc_mult, hidden_size = hidden_states.shape\n    scalar = hidden_size ** -0.5\n\n    output = torch.empty_like(hidden_states)\n\n    if save_for_backward:\n        dot = torch.empty((num_tokens, hc_mult), dtype=torch.float32, device=hidden_states.device)\n        gate_score = torch.empty((num_tokens, hc_mult), dtype=torch.float32, device=hidden_states.device)\n        rstd_x = torch.empty((num_tokens, hc_mult), dtype=torch.float32, device=hidden_states.device)\n        rstd_k = torch.empty((num_tokens, hc_mult), dtype=torch.float32, device=hidden_states.device)\n    else:\n        dot = gate_score = rstd_x = rstd_k = None\n\n    BLOCK_SIZE = triton.next_power_of_2(hidden_size)\n    grid = (num_tokens * hc_mult,)\n\n    _engram_gate_fwd_kernel[grid](\n        hidden_states, k, v, weight_fused,\n        output, dot, gate_score, rstd_x, rstd_k,\n        hc_mult=hc_mult,\n        hidden_size=hidden_size,\n        inv_h=1.0 / hidden_size,\n        eps=eps,\n        clamp_value=clamp_value,\n        scalar=scalar,\n        save_for_backward=save_for_backward,\n        BLOCK_SIZE=BLOCK_SIZE,\n        num_warps=4,\n    )\n\n    return output, dot, gate_score, rstd_x, rstd_k\n```\n\nWait, the speedup with num_warps=4 is 3.32x, with num_warps=2 is 3.33x. os\nos.environ['TILELANG_PRINT_ON_COMPILATION'] = '0'\n\n\n@triton.jit\ndef kernel_bf16_x(\n    x_ptr, k_ptr, v_ptr, w_ptr, out_ptr,\n    dot_ptr, gate_ptr, rstd_x_ptr, rstd_k_ptr,\n    hc_mult: tl.constexpr,\n    hidden_size: tl.constexpr,\n    inv_h, eps, clamp_value, scalar,\n    save_for_backward: tl.constexpr,\n    BLOCK_SIZE: tl.constexpr,\n):\n    pid = tl.program_id(0)\n    token = pid // hc_mult\n    head = pid % hc_mult\n    offs = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_SIZE)\n    mask = offs < hidden_size\n    x_off = token * hc_mult * hidden_size + head * hidden_size\n    # Keep x in bf16, only promote to fp32 when needed\n    x_bf16 = tl.load(x_ptr + x_off + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0)\n    x = x_bf16.to(tl.float32)\n    k_bf16 = tl.load(k_ptr + x_off + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0)\n    k = k_bf16.to(tl.float32)\n    w = tl.load(w_ptr + head * hidden_size + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0)\n    v_bf16 = tl.load(v_ptr + token * hidden_size + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0)\n    v = v_bf16.to(tl.float32)\n    sum_x2 = tl.sum(x * x)\n    sum_k2 = tl.sum(k * k)\n    sum_xkw = tl.sum(x * w * k)\n    rstd_x = tl.rsqrt(sum_x2 * inv_h + eps)\n    rstd_k = tl.rsqrt(sum_k2 * inv_h + eps)\n    scaled_dot = sum_xkw * rstd_x * rstd_k * scalar\n    abs_dot = tl.abs(scaled_dot)\n    sqrt_dot = tl.sqrt(tl.maximum(abs_dot, clamp_value))\n    sign_dot = tl.where(scaled_dot >= 0.0, 1.0, -1.0)\n    gate_score = tl.sigmoid(sign_dot * sqrt_dot)\n    out = x + gate_score * v\n    tl.store(out_ptr + x_off + offs, out.to(tl.bfloat16), mask=mask, cache_modifier='.cs')\n    if save_for_backward:\n        base_idx = token * hc_mult + head\n        tl.store(dot_ptr + base_idx, sum_xkw)\n        tl.store(gate_ptr + base_idx, gate_score)\n        tl.store(rstd_x_ptr + base_idx, rstd_x)\n        tl.store(rstd_k_ptr + base_idx, rstd_k)\n\n\ndef call(x, k, v, w, eps, clamp, save, num_warps, num_stages):\n    num_tokens, hc_mult, hidden_size = x.shape\n    scalar = hidden_size ** -0.5\n    output = torch.empty_like(x)\n    if save:\n        dot = torch.empty((num_tokens, hc_mult), dtype=torch.float32, device=x.device)\n        gate_score = torch.empty((num_tokens, hc_mult), dtype=torch.float32, device=x.device)\n        rstd_x = torch.empty((num_tokens, hc_mult), dtype=torch.float32, device=x.device)\n        rstd_k = torch.empty((num_tokens, hc_mult), dtype=torch.float32, device=x.device)\n    else:\n        dot = gate_score = rstd_x = rstd_k = None\n    BLOCK_SIZE = triton.next_power_of_2(hidden_size)\n    grid = (num_tokens * hc_mult,)\n    kernel_bf16_x[grid](\n        x, k, v, w, output, dot, gate_score, rstd_x, rstd_k,\n        hc_mult=hc_mult, hidden_size=hidden_size,\n        inv_h=1.0/hidden_size, eps=eps, clamp_value=clamp, scalar=scalar,\n        save_for_backward=save, BLOCK_SIZE=BLOCK_SIZE,\n        num_warps=num_warps, num_stages=num_stages,\n    )\n    return output, dot, gate_score, rstd_x, rstd_k\n\n\nfrom Triton should do this automatically.\n\nActually let me also see if the kernel has any wasted work.\n\nLooking at the kernel:\n```python\nsum_x2 = tl.sum(x * x)\nsum_k2 = tl.sum(k * k)\nsum_xkw = tl.sum(x * w * k)\n```\n\nThese three reductions are independent. The compiler should fuse them into a single pass over the data.\n\nHmm, let me check if there's a way to make this even tighter.\n\nActually, the computation `x * x` is redundant with `x * w * k` since we could compute `x` once. But x is already in registers. The compiler should schedule `x*x` and `x*w*k` to use the same `x` load.\n\nOK let me just submit.\n\nWait, let me also think about the multi-warp reduction. With BLOCK_SIZE=4096 and num_warps=4 (128 threads), each thread has 32 elements. The reduction involves:\n- Intra-warp reduction (32 -> 1) using shuffle\n- Cross-warp reduction via SMEM (4 -> 1)\n\nThe cross-warp reduction requires SMEM. Each thread writes its partial sum to SMEM, then warp 0 reads all 4 partial sums and reduces.\n\nThis adds latency. For 3 reductions (sum_x2, sum_k2, sum_xkw), we have 3 cross-warp syncs.\n\nWith num_warps=2 (64 threads), 2 partial sums per reduction. Smaller SMEM traffic.\n\nWith num_warps=8 (256 threads), 8 partial sums. More SMEM traffic.\n\nMaybe num_warps=2 is better because less SMEM traffic. But the benchmark shows similar perf.\n\nOK let me just finalize with num_warps=4 as a reasonable default.\n\nHmm let me also consider: the issue might be that my reduction is too slow. With 4096 elements and small num_warps, each thread does many sequential ops.\n\nLet me check: with num_warps=2 (64 threads), each thread has 64 elements. Reduction: 6 levels (5 intra-warp + 1 cross). Each level is a shuffle + add.\n\nFor 64 elements, each thread does 64 multiplies + 64 adds to compute its partial sum. Then 6 reduction steps.\n\nTotal per thread: 128 fma + 6 shuffle-add. That's a lot of serial work.\n\nWith num_warps=8 (256 threads), each thread has 16 elements. 32 multiplies + 32 adds. Then 8 reduction steps (5 intra + 3 cross).\n\nPer thread: 64 fma + 8 shuffle-add.\n\nSo num_warps=8 has half the serial work per thread but more cross-warp overhead. Net should be similar.\n\nOK let me just go with num_warps=4.\n\nActually wait, let me try one more optimization: explicitly use `tl.fma` or `tl.dot` if available.\n\nActually `tl.dot` is for matrix multiplication. Internally I could allocate one combined tensor and view it 4 ways. But the stride would be 16 bytes, not 4 bytes. Slice [:, 0], [:, 1], etc. gives views of shape (num_tokens*hc_mult,) with stride 4. These are non-contiguous but valid.\n\nThen the grader would receive these non-contiguous views. The grader's correctness check uses calc_diff which casts to fp64 and sums. Non-contiguous tensors work fine for that.\n\nHmm but the test_engram_gate_fwd.py does `assert dot is not None and ...`. At ~1 store per cycle issue rate, that's 131072 cycles / 256 SMs / 16-32 inst/cycle = ~16-32us. Not huge.\n\nIf I combine into 1 store, save ~12-24us. other=0.0).to(tl.float32)\n\n    sum_x2 = tl.sum(x * x)\n    sum_k2 = tl.sum(k * k)\n    sum_xkw = tl.sum(x * w * k)\n\n    rstd_x = tl.rsqrt(sum_x2 * inv_h + eps)\n    rstd_k = tl.rsqrt(sum_k2 * inv_h + eps)\n\n    scaled_dot = sum_xkw * rstd_x * rstd_k * scalar\n    abs_dot = tl.abs(scaled_dot)\n    sqrt_dot = tl.sqrt(tl.maximum(abs_dot, clamp_value))\n    sign_dot = tl.where(scaled_dot >= 0.0, 1.0, -1.0)\n    gate_score = tl.sigmoid(sign_dot * sqrt_dot)\n\n    out = x + gate_score * v\n    tl.store(out_ptr + x_off + offs, out.to(tl.bfloat16), mask=mask, cache_modifier='.cs')\n\n    if save_for_backward:\n        base_idx = token * hc_mult + head\n        tl.store(dot_ptr + base_idx, sum_xkw)\n        tl.store(gate_ptr + base_idx, gate_score)\n        tl.store(rstd_x_ptr + base_idx, rstd_x)\n        tl.store(rstd_k_ptr + base_idx, rstd_k)\n\n\ndef engram_gate_fwd_triton(\n    hidden_states: torch.Tensor,   # (num_tokens, hc_mult, hidden_size), bfloat16\n    k: torch.Tensor,               # (num_tokens, hc_mult, hidden_size), bfloat16\n    v: torch.Tensor,               # (num_tokens, hidden_size), bfloat16\n    weight_fused: torch.Tensor,    # (hc_mult, hidden_size), float32  (= weight_hidden * weight_embed)\n    eps: float,\n    clamp_value: float,\n    save_for_backward: bool = True,\n):\n    \"\"\"Engram gate forward.\n\n    Computes, per (token, head):\n        rstd_x  = rsqrt(mean(x^2, dim=-1) + eps)\n        rstd_k  = rsqrt(mean(k^2, dim=-1) + eps)\n        raw_dot = sum(x * k * weight_fused, dim=-1)\n        dot     = raw_dot * rstd_x * rstd_k * hidden_size**-0.5\n        gate    = sigmoid( sign(dot) * sqrt(clamp_min(|dot|, clamp_value)) )\n        out     = (x + gate * v).bfloat16()          # v is shared across heads\n\n    Returns:\n        (output, dot, gate_score, rstd_x, rstd_k)\n        When save_for_backward is False, the last four are None and only `output`\n        is required to be correct.\n        When True, dot=raw_dot, gate_score, rstd_x, rstd_k are (num_tokens, hc_mult)\n        float32 tensors.\n    \"\"\"\n    num_tokens, hc_mult, hidden_size = hidden_states.shape\n    scalar = hidden_size ** -0.5\n\n    output = torch.empty_like(hidden_states)\n\n    if save_for_backward:\n        dot = torch.empty((num_tokens, hc_mult), dtype=torch.float32, device=hidden_states.device)\n        gate_score = torch.empty((num_tokens, hc_mult), dtype=torch.float32, device=hidden_states.device)\n        rstd_x = torch.empty((num_tokens, hc_mult), dtype=torch.float32, device=hidden_states.device)\n        rstd_k = torch.empty((num_tokens, hc_mult), dtype=torch.float32, device=hidden_states.device)\n    else:\n        dot = gate_score = rstd_x = rstd_k = None\n\n    BLOCK_SIZE = triton.next_power_of_2(hidden_size)\n    grid = (num_tokens * hc_mult,)\n\n    _engram_gate_fwd_kernel[grid](\n        hidden_states, k, v, weight_fused,\n        output, dot, gate_score, rstd_x, rstd_k,\n        hc_mult=hc_mult,\n        hidden_size=hidden_size,\n        inv_h=1.0 / hidden_size,\n        eps=eps,\n        clamp_value=clamp_value,\n        scalar=scalar,\n        save_for_backward=save_for_backward,\n        BLOCK_SIZE=BLOCK_SIZE,\n        num_warps=4,\n    )\n\n    return output, dot, gate_score, rstd_x,
